Script trigger log for mirrorworld.rpg, 07-07-2021 12:05:48

Solid lines '|' show triggered scripts which have already started running but are
waiting or paused due to either another script which was triggered (indicated by a
line to its right) or while waiting for a script they called (not shown).
Dotted lines ':' show triggered scripts which have not even had a chance to start.
(...as above...) means that a script continues waiting multiple ticks for the same reason.

 Symbols in front of script names:
+ -- A script was triggered (queued), possibly also started, possibly also finished
! -- As above, but triggered as a side effect of something the script above it did,
     such as running "close menu", interrupting that script.
     (Note: ! is used only if the command didn't cause an implicit 'wait')
* -- A queued script was started, possibly also finished
- -- A previously started script finished
